manage state, and send notifications:\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe entry point is `AlertNG` (pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go), the main service that initializes and coordinates all alerting components through the `ProvideService()` function.\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (pkg/services/ngalert/store/)\\n\\nThe storage layer is implemented by `DBstore` (pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go), which manages:\\n- **Alert Rules**: CRUD operations for alert rules stored in the database (InsertAlertRules, UpdateAlertRules, DeleteAlertRulesByUID, ListAlertRules)\\n- **Rule Versions**: Tracks rule versions and handles versioning (GetAlertRuleVersions, IncreaseVersionForAllRulesInNamespaces)\\n- **Namespaces**: Manages alert rule groupings (pkg/services/ngalert/store/namespace.go)\\n- **Instances**: Alert instance state storage via InstanceDBStore (pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go)\\n- **Alertmanager Config**: Stores alertmanager configuration (pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go)\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/)\\n\\nThe `schedule` type (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go) with `SchedulerCfg` manages periodic evaluation:\\n- **Alert Rule Scheduling**: Evaluates alert rules on a configurable interval (alert_rule.go, Run())\\n- **Recording Rules**: Executes recording rules to generate time-series data (recording_rule.go)\\n- **Rule Registry**: Maintains in-memory registry of active rules (registry.go)\\n- **Retry Logic**: Handles failed evaluations with exponential backoff (retry.go)\\n- **Jitter**: Distributes rule evaluation across time windows to avoid thundering herd (jitter.go)\\n- **Sequence Processing**: Executes sequences of rules with dependencies\\n\\nThe scheduler fetches rules from DBstore and continuously evaluates them, calling the evaluator for each rule. Results are passed to the state manager for state tracking.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager (pkg/services/ngalert/state/)\\n\\nThe `Manager` (pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go) tracks alert state:\\n- **State Tracking**: Maintains state for each alert instance using in-memory cache (cache.go)\\n- **State Transitions**: Processes evaluation results and manages state changes (ProcessEvalResults())\\n- **State Persistence**: Persists alert state to the database\\n  - Async persistence: persister_async.go (default)\\n  - Sync persistence: persister_sync.go (on-demand)\\n  - Noop persistence: persister_noop.go (disabled)\\n- **State History**: Records alert state transitions to various backends via the Historian\\n- **State Representation**: Maintains `State` objects (state.go) with current state, labels, annotations, firing time, etc.\\n\\nThe manager integrates with the **Historian** (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/core.go) to record state changes:\\n- **Annotation Backend**: Stores history in Grafana annotations (annotation.go)\\n- **Loki Backend**: Writes to Loki logs (loki.go)\\n- **Prometheus Backend**: Writes to remote Prometheus or Mimir via remote write (prometheus.go)\\n- **Query System**: Retrieves historical state for dashboards (query.go)\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/)\\n\\nThe notification system manages alerting:\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager** (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go): Manages per-organization Alertmanager instances\\n- **Alertmanager** (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go): Wraps Prometheus Alertmanager for deduplication, grouping, and routing\\n- **Configuration**: Stores and manages alertmanager routing, receivers, and templates (alertmanager_config.go)\\n- **Crypto**: Encrypts sensitive contact point credentials (crypto.go)\\n- **File Storage**: Persists alertmanager state to disk (file_store.go)\\n- **Receiver Service**: Manages notification receivers/contact points (receiver_svc.go)\\n- **Silence Service**: Manages alert silences and inhibitions (silence_svc.go)\\n- **Legacy Storage**: Compatibility layer for legacy alerting configuration (legacy_storage/persist.go)\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/)\\n\\nThe writer components persist metrics and state:\\n- **PrometheusWriter** (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/prom.go): Writes alert state as time-series metrics to remote Prometheus via remote write protocol\\n- **DataSourceWriter** (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/datasourcewriter.go): Generic writer for persisting evaluation results to external data sources\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup** (pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go:init())\\n   - AlertNG loads configuration and initializes components\\n   - StateManager warms up from historical state via InstanceReader\\n   - AlertsRouter syncs alertmanager config from database\\n\\n2. **Evaluation** (schedule:Run)\\n   - Scheduler fetches alert rules from DBstore periodically\\n   - Rules are evaluated using Evaluator (eval.go)\\n   - Results flow to StateManager.ProcessEvalResults()\\n\\n3. **State Transition** (state/manager.go)\\n   - Manager compares evaluation results with current state\\n   - State transitions are recorded (Normal → Alerting, etc.)\\n   - State is persisted via Persister (async or sync)\\n   - Historian records state transition to configured backend (annotations, Loki, Prometheus)\\n\\n4. **Notification** (sender/router.go)\\n   - AlertsRouter (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go) receives state transitions\\n   - Router routes alerts to MultiOrgAlertmanager\\n   - Alertmanager deduplicates, groups, and routes to receivers\\n   - Contact points send notifications (email, Slack, webhook, etc.)\\n\\n5. **Remote Alerting** (pkg/services/ngalert/remote/)\\n   - Remote alertmanager modes: primary or secondary\\n   - Can sync state to remote Mimir/Cortex via client (client/alertmanager.go, client/mimir.go)\\n\\n## Key Interactions\\n\\n- **Store → Scheduler**: Scheduler.Run() fetches rules from DBstore.ListAlertRules()\\n- **Scheduler → Evaluator**: schedule:alert_rule.go evaluates rules via EvaluatorFactory\\n- **Evaluator → StateManager**: Results passed to Manager.ProcessEvalResults()\\n- **StateManager → Historian**: State transitions written via historian backend\\n- **StateManager → Persister**: Alert state saved to database\\n- **StateManager → AlertsRouter**: State transitions route to notifications\\n- **AlertsRouter → MultiOrgAlertmanager**: Routes alerts to alertmanager instances\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager → Notifier**: Sends notifications via contact points\\n- **Scheduler → Writer**: Recording rules and metrics written via PrometheusWriter\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\n- **API** (pkg/services/ngalert/api/api.go): REST endpoints for rule management, testing, and querying\\n- **Models** (pkg/services/ngalert/models/): Data structures for AlertRule, RuleGroup, Instance, Receiver\\n- **Access Control** (pkg/services/ngalert/accesscontrol/): Role-based access control\\n- **Metrics** (pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/): Prometheus metrics for scheduler, state, and notifications\\n- **Remote** (pkg/services/ngalert/remote/): Support for remote alertmanagers (Mimir, Cortex)\\n- **Provisioning** (pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/): Configuration management via provisioning files\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n- Store alert rule definitions durably\\n- Evaluate rules reliably on a schedule\\n- Track alert state with full history\\n- Send notifications through multiple channels\\n- Support distributed deployments with remote alerting\\n- Provide REST APIs for rule management and History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/)\\n\\nThe writer components persist metrics and state:\\n- **PrometheusWriter** (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/prom.go): Writes alert state as time-series metrics to remote Prometheus via remote write protocol\\n- **DataSourceWriter** (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/datasourcewriter.go): Generic writer for persisting evaluation results to external data sources\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **Startup** (pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go:init())\\n   - AlertNG loads configuration and initializes components\\n   - StateManager warms up from historical state via InstanceReader\\n   - AlertsRouter syncs alertmanager config from database\\n\\n2. **Evaluation** (schedule:Run)\\n   - Scheduler fetches alert rules from DBstore periodically\\n   - Rules are evaluated using Evaluator (eval.go)\\n   - Results flow to StateManager.ProcessEvalResults()\\n\\n3. **State Transition** (state/manager.go)\\n   - Manager compares evaluation results with current state\\n   - State transitions are recorded (Normal → Alerting, etc.)\\n   - State is persisted via Persister (async or sync)\\n   - Historian records state transition to configured backend (annotations, Loki, Prometheus)\\n\\n4. **Notification** (sender/router.go)\\n   - AlertsRouter (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go) receives state transitions\\n   - Router routes alerts to MultiOrgAlertmanager\\n   - Alertmanager deduplicates, groups, and routes to receivers\\n   - Contact points send notifications (email, Slack, webhook, etc.)\\n\\n5. **Remote Alerting** (pkg/services/ngalert/remote/)\\n   - Remote alertmanager modes: primary or secondary\\n   - Can sync state to remote Mimir/Cortex via client (client/alertmanager.go, client/mimir.go)\\n\\n## Key Interactions\\n\\n- **Store → Scheduler**: Scheduler.Run() fetches rules from DBstore.ListAlertRules()\\n- **Scheduler → Evaluator**: schedule:alert_rule.go evaluates rules via EvaluatorFactory\\n- **Evaluator → StateManager**: Results passed to Manager.ProcessEvalResults()\\n- **StateManager → Historian**: State transitions written via historian backend\\n- **StateManager → Persister**: Alert state saved to database\\n- **StateManager → AlertsRouter**: State transitions route to notifications\\n- **AlertsRouter → MultiOrgAlertmanager**: Routes alerts to alertmanager instances\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager → Notifier**: Sends notifications via contact points\\n- **Scheduler → Writer**: Recording rules and metrics written via PrometheusWriter\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\n- **API** (pkg/services/ngalert/api/api.go): REST endpoints for rule management, testing, and querying\\n- **Models** (pkg/services/ngalert/models/): Data structures for AlertRule, RuleGroup, Instance, Receiver\\n- **Access Control** (pkg/services/ngalert/accesscontrol/): Role-based access control\\n- **Metrics** (pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/): Prometheus metrics for scheduler, state, and notifications\\n- **Remote** (pkg/services/ngalert/remote/): Support for remote alertmanagers (Mimir, Cortex)\\n- **Provisioning** (pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/): Configuration management via provisioning files\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n- Store alert rule definitions durably\\n- Evaluate rules reliably on a schedule\\n- Track alert state with full history\\n- Send notifications through multiple channels\\n- Support distributed deployments with remote alerting\\n- Provide REST APIs for rule management and dashboards\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
